<tr>
<td style="line-height:normal;padding:6px 5px 3px;text-align:center"><div class="plainlinks hlist navbar"><span style="word-spacing:0">This diagram: </span><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:Manchester_Central_Metrolink_lines" title="Template:Manchester Central Metrolink lines"><span title="View this template">view</span></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:Manchester_Central_Metrolink_lines" title="Template talk:Manchester Central Metrolink lines"><span title="Discuss this template">talk</span></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Manchester_Central_Metrolink_lines&amp;action=edit"><span title="Edit this template">edit</span></a></li></ul></div>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
</td></tr>
</tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The Piccadilly <a href="/wiki/Manchester_Metrolink" title="Manchester Metrolink">Metrolink</a> tram stop is located at ground level in the <a href="/wiki/Undercroft" title="Undercroft">undercroft</a> underneath the main line station; an area of the station which was historically used for <a href="/wiki/Warehouse" title="Warehouse">warehousing</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-archive_9-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-archive-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> it is one of nine stops serving <a href="/wiki/Manchester_city_centre" title="Manchester city centre">Manchester city centre</a>, within the system's <a href="/wiki/Zone_1_(Manchester_Metrolink)" title="Zone 1 (Manchester Metrolink)">Zone 1</a>. Trams enter the stop from the streets in each direction via short tunnels. There are two platforms, one for trams towards <a href="/wiki/Etihad_Campus_tram_stop" title="Etihad Campus tram stop">Etihad Campus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ashton-under-Lyne_tram_stop" title="Ashton-under-Lyne tram stop">Ashton-under-Lyne</a> , and one for trams towards <a href="/wiki/Bury_Interchange" title="Bury Interchange">Bury</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eccles_Interchange" title="Eccles Interchange">Eccles</a> and <a href="/wiki/Altrincham_Interchange" title="Altrincham Interchange">Altrincham</a>. There are steps, lifts and escalators between the platform level and a <a href="/wiki/Mezzanine" title="Mezzanine">mezzanine</a> level, along with further steps, lifts and escalators that connect with the main line station's concourse. There are also multiple entrances present at ground level from the surrounding streets.<sup id="cite_ref-LRTACC_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LRTACC-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Piccadilly_tram_entrance_from_London_Road.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Piccadilly_tram_entrance_from_London_Road.jpg/220px-Piccadilly_tram_entrance_from_London_Road.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="180" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Piccadilly_tram_entrance_from_London_Road.jpg/330px-Piccadilly_tram_entrance_from_London_Road.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/43/Piccadilly_tram_entrance_from_London_Road.jpg/440px-Piccadilly_tram_entrance_from_London_Road.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4344" data-file-height="3560" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Piccadilly_tram_entrance_from_London_Road.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A tram entering Piccadilly from London Road. The tram station is located below the rail platforms in the undercroft.</div></div></div>
<p>On 20 July 1992, the tram station was first opened, originally being known as <i>Piccadilly Undercroft</i>. As the stop was located directly underneath the main line station platforms, the then station operator <a href="/wiki/British_Rail" title="British Rail">British Rail</a> required that it be built inside a protective concrete box, in order to protect the cast iron supports for the main line platforms from the possibility of collision or fire damage.<sup id="cite_ref-LRTACC_57-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LRTACC-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-thetrams_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-thetrams-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As Piccadilly originally served as a terminus of the system, early operations saw one platform being used for arrivals from Altrincham, Bury, and later Eccles, and the other platform was used for departures. Empty trams ran from the arrival platform into a nearby <a href="/wiki/Reversing_siding" class="mw-redirect" title="Reversing siding">reversing siding</a> in a tunnel, where they would reverse and then enter the departure platform. From the onset, the stop had been designed with future extension in mind; as such, since the opening of the <a href="/wiki/East_Manchester_Line" title="East Manchester Line">extension towards Ashton</a> in 2013, the former arrivals platform has also been used for departures towards Ashton as well as terminating trams, while the former departures platform also handles arrivals from Ashton. Terminating trams use a reversing siding on the Ashton line between Piccadilly and New Islington tram stops.<sup id="cite_ref-LRTACC_57-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LRTACC-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-thetrams_58-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-thetrams-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During 2008, the tram station was refurbished, after which it became the first station to display the new Metrolink corporate identity.<sup id="cite_ref-hemisphere_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hemisphere-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Station signage bears the yellow and silver livery as applied to the new generation of trams since 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-MEN-design_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MEN-design-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>According to TfGM, the Piccadilly tram station is one of the most frequented stops on the Metrolink network.<sup id="cite_ref-TfGM_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TfGM-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Metrolink_services">Metrolink services</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Manchester_Piccadilly_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Metrolink services">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As of 2019, Manchester Piccadilly stop is the terminus for Metrolink services to <a href="/wiki/Bury_Interchange" title="Bury Interchange">Bury</a> and <a href="/wiki/Altrincham_tram_stop" class="mw-redirect" title="Altrincham tram stop">Altrincham</a>, and a major stop on the through services between <a href="/wiki/Eccles_Interchange" title="Eccles Interchange">Eccles</a> and <a href="/wiki/MediaCityUK_tram_stop" title="MediaCityUK tram stop">MediaCityUK</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ashton-under-Lyne_tram_stop" title="Ashton-under-Lyne tram stop">Ashton-under-Lyne</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Services mostly run every 12 minutes on all routes.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
